The following outline is a representation of the [XML format](https://github.com/usnistgov/OSCAL/blob/v1.0.1/xml/schema/oscal_assessment-plan_schema.xsd) for this [model](/concepts/layer/assessment/assessment-plan/). For each element or attribute, the name links to the corresponding entry in the [XML Format Reference](../xml-reference/). The cardinality and data type are also provided for each element or attribute where appropriate.

                              <div class="OM-choices">
                                 <p class="OM-lit">A choice of:</p>
